info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family

posted:Posted May 3, 2024
msg:The room is spacious. Three people can live in one room and stack a lot of items without feeling cramped. There is a wide balcony and clothes drying rack, which is very friendly to mothers who like to wash clothes when going out.
The sound insulation effect is poor. There are many people staying on holidays, and the sound of closing doors and talking outside the door can be heard. At night, the frogs outside the balcony are croaking one after another, which is also good as white noise.
The service attitude of the hotel staff is very good, and they have a strong sense of proactive service. The staff responsible for check-in learned that I wanted to take a hot spring bath, and they were very enthusiastic to guide and handle it, and also gave me fruits. Free lemonade is placed in the hall, and some staff also take the initiative to hand over water. I donâ€™t know how to adjust the air conditioning temperature, and someone will come to the door soon after calling the service phone.
There are many projects for children to play, including childrenâ€™s playground (at their own expense), swimming pool (with bubbles), and childrenâ€™s movies are shown at night. My son had a lot of fun.
Overall, it is a cost-effective hotel suitable for staying with the elderly and children.
